    SELECT TOP(1) [f].[Id], [f].[CommunityId], [f].[CreatedBy], [f].[CreatedDate], [f].[FacilityDetails], [f].[FacilityLocation], [f].[FacilityName], [f].[FacilityTypeId], [f].[Rate], [f].[UpdatedBy], [f].[UpdatedDate], [f0].[Id] AS [Id0], [f0].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy0], [f0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [f0].[Name], [f0].[UpdatedBy] AS [UpdatedBy0], [f0].[UpdatedDate] AS [UpdatedDate0], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[Address], [c].[CityName], [c].[CommunityId] AS [CommunityId0], [c].[CommunityName], [c].[CommunityTypeId], [c].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy1], [c].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate1], [c].[FeesMonthly], [c].[GracePeriod], [c].[NoOfParkingLot], [c].[NoOfUnits], [c].[PICEmail], [c].[PICMobile], [c].[PICName], [c].[StateId], [c].[UpdatedBy] AS [UpdatedBy1], [c].[UpdatedDate] AS [UpdatedDate1]
    FROM [Facility] AS [f]
    INNER JOIN [FacilityType] AS [f0] ON [f].[FacilityTypeId] = [f0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Community] AS [c] ON [f].[CommunityId] = [c].[Id]
    WHERE [f].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [FacilityPhoto] AS [f1] ON [t].[Id] = [f1].[FacilityId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1]

    SELECT TOP(1) [f].[Id], [f].[CommunityId], [f].[CreatedBy], [f].[CreatedDate], [f].[FacilityDetails], [f].[FacilityLocation], [f].[FacilityName], [f].[FacilityTypeId], [f].[Rate], [f].[UpdatedBy], [f].[UpdatedDate], [f0].[Id] AS [Id0], [f0].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy0], [f0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [f0].[Name], [f0].[UpdatedBy] AS [UpdatedBy0], [f0].[UpdatedDate] AS [UpdatedDate0], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[Address], [c].[CityName], [c].[CommunityId] AS [CommunityId0], [c].[CommunityName], [c].[CommunityTypeId], [c].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy1], [c].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate1], [c].[FeesMonthly], [c].[GracePeriod], [c].[NoOfParkingLot], [c].[NoOfUnits], [c].[PICEmail], [c].[PICMobile], [c].[PICName], [c].[StateId], [c].[UpdatedBy] AS [UpdatedBy1], [c].[UpdatedDate] AS [UpdatedDate1]
